[30;1m58 | [0m[35mPython's `file` objects. In the same way that file objects abstract a[0m
[30;1m59 | [0m[35msingle file, FS objects abstract an entire filesystem.[0m
[30;1m60 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m61 | [0m[35mLet's look at a simple piece of code as an example. The following[0m
[30;1m62 | [0m[35mfunction uses the PyFilesystem API to count the number of non-blank[0m
[30;1m63 | [0m[35mlines of Python code in a directory. It works _recursively_, so it will[0m
[30;1m64 | [0m[35mfind `.py` files in all sub-directories.[0m
